Crypto.Hash.IO

Description

Generalized impure cryptographic hash interface

Documentation
=============

class[HashAlgorithm](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-Hash-IO.html) a where[Source](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/src/Crypto.Hash.Types.html#HashAlgorithm)[#](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-Hash-IO.html#t:HashAlgorithm)

Class representing hashing algorithms.

The interface presented here is update in place and lowlevel. the Hash module takes care of hidding the mutable interface properly.

Associated Types

data[MutableContext](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-Hash-IO.html) a [Source](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/src/Crypto.Hash.IO.html#MutableContext)[#](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-Hash-IO.html#t:MutableContext)

A Mutable hash context

This type is an instance of `ByteArrayAccess` for debugging purpose. Internal layout is architecture dependent, may contain uninitialized data fragments, and change in future versions. The bytearray should not be used as input to cryptographic algorithms.

#### Instances

Instances details
